[HUMAN]: Windows 11 build 27813 vs Windows 11 24H2 vs Windows 11 23H2 vs Windows 10 22H2, Pros and Cons for modern PCs?

[AI]: Okay, here's a breakdown of Windows 11 build 27813, Windows 11 24H2, Windows 11 23H2, and Windows 10 22H2 for modern PCs as of today, June 20, 2025:

**Windows 11 Build 27813 (Canary Channel)**

This is a very early, experimental build.  It's primarily focused on under-the-hood improvements and bug fixes rather than introducing major new features [neowin].  Here's what you need to know:

*   **Pros:**
    *   Includes fixes for audio crashes related to MIDI updates and the WDMAud system driver [5, 13, 23, 27, 28, 41].
    *   Addresses display issues where color profiles might not be listed correctly in Settings > System > Display > Color Management [5, 13, 23, 27, 28, 41].
    *   General improvements to enhance the overall experience [5, 13, 23, 27, 28, 41].
*   **Cons:**
    *   The Location History feature (used by Cortana) has been removed, which might be a drawback for some users [neowin, reddit, logicstechnology, winaero, windows, technine].
    *   Joining the Canary Channel on Copilot+ PCs from other channels might cause loss of Windows Hello PIN and biometric login options [5, 13, 23, 28, 41, windows, reddit, neowin, technine, logicstechnology].  A workaround is to recreate the PIN [reddit, neowin, logicstechnology].
    *   A persistent crash related to `d3d9.dll` may affect application launches [5, 13, 23, 24, 28, 41, windows, logicstechnology, reddit, neowin].

**Who is this for?**  This build is really only suitable for enthusiasts and developers who are comfortable with frequent updates and potential instability.  It's not recommended for a primary, production machine.

**Windows 11 24H2**

This is the most current generally available feature update for Windows 11. It began rolling out in June 2024 for Copilot Plus PCs and October 1, 2024, for all users [2, wikipedia].

*   **Pros:**
    *   **New Features:**  It includes a wide array of new features, including a new account manager experience on the Start menu [2, 11, wikipedia], Emoji 15.1 support [2, wikipedia], the ability to back up and restore sound settings via Windows Backup [2, wikipedia], redesigned dialogs, Task Manager improvements [2], improvements to the Windows share window [2, wikipedia], Voice access improvements [2, 7, wikipedia], HDR background support [2, 8, 34, pcmag], Wi-Fi 7 support [2, 9, 18, acer, wikipedia], Bluetooth LE Audio support [2, 9, 18, microsoft, acer], search for documents and photos using descriptive phrases [2, wikipedia], Auto Super Resolution (on Copilot+ PCs) [2, 18, wikipedia], Windows Recall (preview) on Copilot+ PCs [2], Share to Android [8, pcmag], Sudo for Windows [8, 34, pcmag], Widgets Updates [8], Unified Teams App [8, pcmag], Voice Focus [8, pcmag], streamlined File Explorer [8, 9, 10, 34], smart power management [9], and the ability to join and share Wi-Fi networks with QR codes [9, microsoft].
    *   **Security:** Part of the Windows kernel has been rewritten in Rust [18, acer].
*   **Cons:**
    *   **System Requirements:** Requires a x86-64-v2 CPU supporting SSE4.2 and POPCNT CPU instructions [2, wikipedia].
    *   **Known Issues:** May have broken biometrics and camera support on some devices [wikipedia]. Some older games and applications may not function properly [2, wikipedia].
    *   **Performance:**  May allocate more memory than 23H2 [4, 21]. Some users have reported performance issues with Intel Core Ultra 9 285K processors [16, 25, 33, laptopmag, neowin, techradar]. May have worse latency than Windows 10 22H2 [39].
    *   **Compatibility Holds:**  Several compatibility holds are in place due to driver issues, particularly with `sprotect.sys` (used by some security software) [borncity, bleepingcomputer, microsoft, theregister, windowsforum, zdnet, reddit], Easy Anti-Cheat [microsoft, windowscentral, easeus], Intel Smart Sound Technology (SST) drivers [zdnet, microsoft], and Dirac Audio [microsoft, techrepublic, reddit, windowscentral, bleepingcomputer, windowsforum, theregister, easeus, microsoft].  These holds prevent affected devices from being offered the update.  There are also issues with some wallpaper customization applications [theregister], Auto HDR [microsoft], Google Workspace Sync [microsoft], and Autodesk AutoCAD 2022 [microsoft].

**Who is this for?**  Most users with modern PCs *that meet the minimum requirements* should upgrade to 24H2 to take advantage of the latest features and security improvements.  *However*, it's crucial to check for compatibility issues with your hardware and software, especially if you use specialized security software or play games with Easy Anti-Cheat.  Make sure your drivers are up to date *before* upgrading.

**Windows 11 23H2**

This was the previous feature update to 24H2, released in October 2023 [2, 7, wikipedia, microsoft].

*   **Pros:**
    *   Introduced a modernized File Explorer [7, 14, 15, 20, wikipedia], the ability to never combine taskbar buttons [7, 14, 15, 20], Outlook for Windows Preview as an inbox app [7, wikipedia], improvements to refresh rate logic for multiple monitors [7], Windows Copilot [7, 10, 14, 15, 20, wikipedia], Windows Backup with a new look and feature set [7, 15, 20, wikipedia], passkey support via Windows Hello [7, 15, wikipedia], a "System" label for system apps in the Start Menu [7, wikipedia], Dynamic Lighting for RGB control [14, 15, 20, starwindsoftware, pureinfotech], native RAR, 7-zip, TAR, and GZ support [14, 15, 20, beebom, pureinfotech], a new volume mixer [10, 14], and suggested Snap Layouts [7].
*   **Cons:**
    *   In some cases, upgrading from 23H2 to 24H2 can result in performance regressions [4, 21, neowin].
    *   Some users have reported game stutters or FPS drops after upgrading to Windows 11 23H2 [17, partitionwizard].
    *   Some users have reported CPU performance degradation after updating to 23H2, which can be resolved by enabling Memory Integrity under Core Isolation settings [35, reddit].

**Who is this for?**  If you are currently running 23H2 and not experiencing any issues, and are concerned about potential compatibility problems with 24H2, you *could* remain on 23H2 for the time being.  However, you'll eventually want to upgrade to continue receiving security updates.  Make sure you are on at least the May 2024 nonsecurity preview update before attempting to upgrade to 24H2 [37, microsoft].

**Windows 10 22H2**

This is the latest and final version of Windows 10 [32, 42, windowscentral].  It was released in October 2022 [11, 29, 32, 42, thurrott, wikipedia].

*   **Pros:**
    *   Generally offers quality improvements, bug fixes, and security updates [26, 32, 43].
    *   Some users find it smoother and more responsive than Windows 11, especially on older hardware [22, 46].
*   **Cons:**
    *   Windows 10 is in maintenance mode, with no major new features being added [32, 42, windowscentral].
    *   Some users have reported lackluster gaming performance [40, 45, partitionwizard].

**Who is this for?**  Windows 10 22H2 is a good choice for users who prefer a more familiar interface and want a stable, reliable operating system.  It's also a viable option for older hardware that may not meet the minimum requirements for Windows 11.  *However*, keep in mind that Windows 10 will reach its end of life on October 14, 2025, after which it will no longer receive security updates.

**General Recommendations for all OS**

*   **Keep Drivers Updated:**  This is crucial for optimal performance and compatibility [6].
*   **Clean Install vs. In-Place Upgrade:** Performance can vary between clean installs and in-place upgrades [4, 21, 33, neowin]. A clean install is generally recommended for the best performance, but it's more time-consuming.
*   **Backup:**  Always create a backup of your system before making major changes, such as upgrading the operating system [microsoft, youtube].
*   **Check Compatibility:** Before upgrading to a new version of Windows, check for known compatibility issues with your hardware and software. The Windows Release Health Dashboard is a good resource for this [windowsforum, bleepingcomputer].

I hope this comprehensive comparison helps you make the best decision for your modern PC!

--- Research Result 3 ---
Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent, credible information on the specified topic and synthesize it into a verifiable text artifact.

Based on the search results, here's a summary of the driver issues and compatibility holds present in Windows 11 24H2, particularly those related to `sprotect.sys` and Easy Anti-Cheat, along with available workarounds:

**1. sprotect.sys Driver Issues:**

*   **Problem:** Windows 11 24H2 has a compatibility issue with the `sprotect.sys` driver, which is used by specialized security software and enterprise solutions for encryption protection. [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) This issue can cause affected devices to become unresponsive and display a blue or black screen error (BSOD). [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) The driver can be automatically installed with various applications. [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) The issue impacts all versions of the `sprotect.sys` driver (1.0.2.372 and 1.0.3.48903). [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)
*   **Affected Users:** Users running security or enterprise software using SenseShield Technology's `sprotect.sys` driver. [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
*   **Safeguard Hold:** Microsoft has applied a compatibility hold, preventing affected devices from receiving the Windows 11 24H2 update via Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6)
*   **Workaround:**
    *   Do not manually update to version 24H2 using the Windows 11 Installation Assistant or the media creation tool until the issue is resolved. [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    *   IT admins can check safeguard ID: 56318982 in Windows Update for Business reports to identify impacted systems. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    *   Check for safeguard holds by going to Start > Settings > Windows Update and selecting "Check for Windows updates." [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) If your device has an upgrade block, you'll see a message. [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
*   **Resolution:** Microsoft is working with SenseShield Technology Co. to resolve the compatibility issue. [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)

**2. Easy Anti-Cheat (EAC) Issues:**

*   **Problem:** An incompatibility exists between Windows 11 24H2 and the Easy Anti-Cheat application, a software automatically installed with some games to prevent cheating. This can cause devices to stop responding and display a blue screen with a "MEMORY\_MANAGEMENT" error. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Affected Users:** Primarily affects gamers, especially those playing games like Asphalt 8, Apex Legends, and Fortnite. The issue is more prevalent on devices with Intel's Alder Lake+ processors and vPro platform, using Easy Anti-Cheat drivers released before April 2024. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Safeguard Hold:** Microsoft has applied a compatibility hold on devices running incompatible Easy Anti-Cheat drivers, preventing them from receiving the update through Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Workaround:**
    *   Do not manually update to version 24H2 using the Windows 11 Installation Assistant or the media creation tool until the issue is resolved. [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    *   Update your games. [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) A game update might include a compatible Easy Anti-Cheat version. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)
*   **Resolution:**
    *   Microsoft released an emergency out-of-band update (KB5063060) to address this incompatibility, which may be installed automatically. [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)
    *   If KB5063060 doesn't install automatically, it can be downloaded manually from the Microsoft Update Catalog.

**3. Other Compatibility Holds and Issues:**

*   **Intel Smart Sound Technology (SST) Drivers:** Blue screen errors can occur on devices with Intel 11th Gen Core processors and specific versions (10.29.0.5152 or 10.30.0.5152) of Intel SST drivers. [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-13) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) The resolution is to update the Intel SST drivers to version 10.30.00.5714 or later, or 10.29.00.5714 or later via Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)
*   **Dirac Audio:** Devices containing Dirac Audio with `cridspapo.dll` may experience audio output issues. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [techrepublic](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-14) A compatibility hold is in place. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [techrepublic](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-14) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
*   **Wallpaper Customization Applications:** Incompatibility with some wallpaper customization applications can cause wallpapers not appearing correctly, icons disappearing, and other issues. [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) Microsoft is gradually lifting the safeguard hold as developers release updates. [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) Workarounds include updating the wallpaper app or uninstalling it before updating to Windows 11 24H2.
*   **Auto HDR:** Devices that have enabled Auto HDR are blocked from installing Windows 11, version 24H2. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) The workaround is to turn off Auto HDR on your device. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
*   **Google Workspace Sync:** Devices using Google Workspace Sync are blocked from installing Windows 11, version 24H2. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) The resolution is to install the latest version of Google Workspace Sync (4.3.68.0). [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
*   **Autodesk AutoCAD 2022:** After installing Windows 11, version 24H2, all versions of Autodesk AutoCAD 2022 might not open on some devices. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)

**General Recommendations:**

*   Do not attempt to manually update to Windows 11 24H2 using the Installation Assistant or Media Creation Tool if you are affected by any of the compatibility holds. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
*   Check the Windows Release Health Dashboard for the latest information on known issues and safeguard holds. [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
*   Keep your drivers and applications updated to the latest versions.
*   If you encounter issues after updating, consider rolling back to the previous version of Windows. [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)

Microsoft is actively working to resolve these issues and is collaborating with relevant vendors to provide fixes.

[borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) This issue can cause affected devices to become unresponsive and display a blue or black screen error (BSOD). [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) The driver can be automatically installed with various applications. [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) The issue impacts all versions of the `sprotect.sys` driver (1.0.2.372 and 1.0.3.48903). [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)\n*   **Affected Users:** Users running security or enterprise software using SenseShield Technology's `sprotect.sys` driver. [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)\n*   **Safeguard Hold:** Microsoft has applied a compatibility hold, preventing affected devices from receiving the Windows 11 24H2 update via Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6)\n*   **Workaround:**\n    *   Do not manually update to version 24H2 using the Windows 11 Installation Assistant or the media creation tool until the issue is resolved. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)\n    *   Check for safeguard holds by going to Start > Settings > Windows Update and selecting \"Check for Windows updates.\" [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) If your device has an upgrade block, you'll see a message. Easy Anti-Cheat (EAC) Issues:**\n\n*   **Problem:** An incompatibility exists between Windows 11 24H2 and the Easy Anti-Cheat application, a software automatically installed with some games to prevent cheating. This can cause devices to stop responding and display a blue screen with a \"MEMORY\\_MANAGEMENT\" error. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)\n*   **Affected Users:** Primarily affects gamers, especially those playing games like Asphalt 8, Apex Legends, and Fortnite. The issue is more prevalent on devices with Intel's Alder Lake+ processors and vPro platform, using Easy Anti-Cheat drivers released before April 2024. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)\n*   **Safeguard Hold:** Microsoft has applied a compatibility hold on devices running incompatible Easy Anti-Cheat drivers, preventing them from receiving the update through Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)\n*   **Workaround:**\n    *   Do not manually update to version 24H2 using the Windows 11 Installation Assistant or the media creation tool until the issue is resolved. [borncity](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)\n    *   Update your games. [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) A game update might include a compatible Easy Anti-Cheat version. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)\n*   **Resolution:**\n    *   Microsoft released an emergency out-of-band update (KB5063060) to address this incompatibility, which may be installed automatically. [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [windowslatest](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)\n    *   If KB5063060 doesn't install automatically, it can be downloaded manually from the Microsoft Update Catalog.\n\n**3. Other Compatibility Holds and Issues:**\n\n*   **Intel Smart Sound Technology (SST) Drivers:** Blue screen errors can occur on devices with Intel 11th Gen Core processors and specific versions (10.29.0.5152 or 10.30.0.5152) of Intel SST drivers. [zdnet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-13) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) The resolution is to update the Intel SST drivers to version 10.30.00.5714 or later, or 10.29.00.5714 or later via Windows Update. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)\n*   **Dirac Audio:** Devices containing Dirac Audio with `cridspapo.dll` may experience audio output issues. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [techrepublic](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-14) A compatibility hold is in place. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [windowscentral](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [bleepingcomputer](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [windowsforum](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [easeus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [techrepublic](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-14) [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)\n*   **Wallpaper Customization Applications:** Incompatibility with some wallpaper customization applications can cause wallpapers not appearing correctly, icons disappearing, and other issues. [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) Microsoft is gradually lifting the safeguard hold as developers release updates. [theregister](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) Workarounds include updating the wallpaper app or uninstalling it before updating to Windows 11 24H2.\n*   **Auto HDR:** Devices that have enabled Auto HDR are blocked from installing Windows 11, version 24H2. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) The workaround is to turn off Auto HDR on your device. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)\n*   **Google Workspace Sync:** Devices using Google Workspace Sync are blocked from installing Windows 11, version 24H2. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) The resolution is to install the latest version of Google Workspace Sync (4.3.68.0). [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)\n*   **Autodesk AutoCAD 2022:** After installing Windows 11, version 24H2, all versions of Autodesk AutoCAD 2022 might not open on some devices. [microsoft](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)\n\n**General Recommendations:**\n\n*   Do not attempt to manually update to Windows 11 24H2 using the Installation Assistant or Media Creation Tool if you are affected by any of the compatibility holds.
